You ever wonder why there isn't more of this beautiful kind of acoustic music flowing through the airwaves? The human condition is injured and in pain. This kind of melody strips away the trappings of society and bares the wires of your soul. Just a simple melody can cut very deep, when the wounds are so fresh. Seems much easier to drown ones soul with layers and layers of over produced drivel...to avoid the emotions attached with the music. I, myself, love to wallow in the deepest places these melodies take me. Thanks again, Ed, for taking me to church today. Great stuff.
